```python
    455 |  # node_mean_3
           %"mean_3"<FLOAT,[1,1280,1,1]> ⬅️ ::ReduceMean(%"gelu_53", %"val_787"{[-1, -2]}) {noop_with_empty_axes=0, keepdims=1}
    456 |  # node_view_16
           %"view_16"<FLOAT,[1,1280]> ⬅️ ::Reshape(%"mean_3", %"val_791"{[1, 1280]}) {allowzero=1}
    457 |  # node_Gemm_1040
           %"linear_8"<FLOAT,[1,512]> ⬅️ ::Gemm(%"view_16", %"trunk.head.fc.weight"{...}) {beta=1.0, transB=1, alpha=1.0, transA=0}
    return %"linear_8"<FLOAT,[1,512]>
}


```
